 That is why he cannot come to India for muscle

 Sikkim came into existence in 1642, when Phuntansong Namgyal was declared the first Chogyal (king) of Sikkim
 namagyal ko teen buddha bhikshuon ne raja ghoshit kiya tha

 bhartiya sena ne rajmahal ko chaaron taraf se gher rakhaa tha

 iske baad chogyal ko unke mahal main hi nazarband kar diya gaya

 janamat sangrah main 97
